name:T‚Äço‚Äçm
info:Superior 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:2.7
posted:Posted February 15, 2024
msg:It is a five-star hotel with a long history. During the Chinese New Year, a twin room only costs more than HK$300. In addition, the hotel rating is probably the lowest among Zhongshan star hotels, so it is expected that the price will be low.
The room facilities are outdated, it's like going back in time thirty years. As soon as we arrived on the floor, there was already a musty smell. When we entered the room, the musty smell was even stronger. All the metal handles and drains in the room have been oxidized, the headboard has obvious stains, the drain in the bathroom is leaking, there is always a pool of water on the floor, etc...
Reporting to the front desk staff that there is a problem with the room, asking for a room transfer is of course the standard response. The room is full and cannot be arranged, and it is emphasized that there is no problem with these rooms.
To be fair, some rooms in the hotel have been renovated, so there is no big problem in staying in these rooms. However, it is strongly recommended not to rent out such unrenovated rooms to guests anymore. The few hundred dollars received will definitely not make up for the negative impact on the hotel. I believe that guests who have never stayed in such rooms will stay again. The country has developed rapidly in the past few decades. It is a pity that we still encounter this kind of management and arrogant front desk staff today. Although everyone has different positioning, the experience is much worse than staying in other vibrant cultural hotels.
The location of the hotel is excellent. I also went to have tea on the fourth floor. The garden there is very well maintained. I believe the hotel is still capable of running this hotel well. I hope it will not follow the footsteps of the Fuhua Hotel.
Another thing worth praising is that although the room facilities are old, the bed sheets, pillow bags, etc. are still of a high standard, and the quality and cleanliness are also very good.

name:L‚ÄçA‚ÄçU
info:Boutique Room
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 28, 2023
msg:20230526_50+ Zhongshan trip Zhongshan International Hotel

Zhongshan International Hotel is not only the first stop of this itinerary, but also the accommodation hotel for two nights. Last month, through the online platform, I booked a boutique room for 2 nights from June 26 to 28 at HK$608. After getting off the bus, I went to the hotel to check in. Although it was 3 hours before the check-in time, the room was still allocated early.

The non-smoking room has an area of 22 square meters. Although it is not very spacious, it has more usable space than ordinary boutique hotels. In addition to the double bed, there are desks, sofas, and large windows facing the street. The bathroom is also It is a wet and dry separation design.

When collecting information, many netizens claimed that the hotel had been completed for some time and the facilities were dilapidated. But after checking in, this old-style 5-star hotel is not flashy, the hot water is hot, the air-conditioning is cold enough, and the sanitation is in place. There are restaurants, restaurants, Japanese restaurants, shopping malls, and health centers on the 4th floor above the ground. , swimming pool, fitness room, for the residents, what more can you ask for.

I remember traveling in Guangzhou earlier and staying in a newer hotel, which only had a bathroom glass door that was not practical in appearance, and the washbasin was designed in an external room. Perhaps young people would be greedy for new ideas. But for a place that is only used as a place to rest after playing, it is inevitable to give people a sense of putting the cart before the horse.

Cost performance has always been the primary consideration when choosing a hotel to stay in. Even though the nearby 2-star hotel not only charges cheaper, but also provides buffet breakfast, but the online reviews are also poor, and there is no outdoor swimming pool in the international hotel. In the hot summer, the outdoor swimming pool is undoubtedly a major selling point to attract residents, so we chose the old over the new.

This short trip has a very pleasant impression. I will definitely stay again next time. It is a hotel worth recommending.
